**Minifigure Group 1 (Harry Potter):**
- Attach hair to head, head to torso, and torso to legs.
- Add brown wand to right hand and coin to left hand.
- Dress Harry in black pants, gray vest, black jacket with red lapels, white collared shirt, and red tie.
- Harry has unruly black hair and thin-rimmed glasses.

**Sub-build 1 (Road Sign to Hogwarts):**
1. Place green 4x4 circular plate.
2. Add dark gray 2x2 circular tile with single stud.
3. Attach green 1x1 plate with three leaves on each side.
4. Stack candles four high on the tile.
5. Put lantern frame on top of the candles.
6. Create sign board for "Hogsmeade" and "Hogwarts."

**Main-Build 1 (Steam Locomotive):**
1. Build locomotive frame with dark gray bricks.
2. Add axles for driving wheels.
3. Attach plates for tender connection.

LEGO Building Instructions: Bag 1 and 2, Book 1

1. Police Officer Minifigure:
- Use dark blue legs, light blue torso, and female head to assemble the police officer.
- Attach clear visor to white helmet and place it on the minifigure's head.
- Put handcuffs in the minifigure's hand.

2. Crook Minifigure:
- Build the crook with black legs, striped torso, male head, and black cap.
- Place money in the crook's hand.

3. Police Bike:
- Combine black bike underframe with white bike frame.
- Add white 1x2 plate with clip to the bike.
- Attach handlebar and trans-light blue tile.
- Insert cylinders into black tires and attach them to the bike.

4. Crook Car (Part 1):
- Construct car frame, plates, bricks, and steering wheel as directed.

5. Crook Car (Part 2):
- Continue building the car by adding plates, tiles, and spoiler.

6. Wheels:
- Insert cylinders into tires and attach them to the car.

Congratulations on completing the crook's car! Place the crook behind the steering wheel and enjoy the ride while avoiding the police officer.
